## Our Comprehensive Eye Services

### Key Treatments

![Dr. Nikhil Nasta - Best Childen's Eye Doctor in Khar](https://static.wixstatic.com/media/1231c0_9a95edc645ea4c258d07200a0cab010f~mv2.webp/v1/fill/w_144,h_192,al_c,q_80,usm_0.66_1.00_0.01,blur_2,enc_avif,quality_auto/81a8e76a-64c6-467f-9d2e-15f3ca7e2d03.webp)

* Lasik Surgery  
Freedom from glasses and contact lenses is possible with our advanced LASIK procedures. Using the sophisticated Contoura Lasik system, we create a precise map of your eye's surface to guide the laser treatment. This personalized approach allows us to address even subtle vision imperfections, providing clearer vision and reduced dependence on corrective lenses. The procedure is quick and comfortable, with most patients returning to their normal activities within a day or two.  
​  
[See More Details](https://www.eyesurgeonmumbai.com/lasik-surgery-mumbai)
* Cataract Surgery  
When the natural lens of your eye becomes cloudy with age, daily activities like reading and driving can become challenging. Our advanced No Patch - No Stitch - No Injection cataract surgery offers a comfortable solution using the state-of-the-art Alcon Laureate World Phaco System. During this precise microsurgical procedure, we gently remove the clouded lens and replace it with a crystal-clear artificial lens. Patients typically experience improved vision within days, and many are amazed by the vivid colors and clarity they regain. We offer various premium lens options, including multifocal and toric lenses, that can reduce or eliminate the need for glasses after surgery.  
​  
[See More Details](https://www.eyesurgeonmumbai.com/cataract-surgery-mumbai)
* Glaucoma Treatment  
Glaucoma, often called the "silent thief of sight," can cause irreversible vision loss without early intervention. Our glaucoma care combines careful monitoring with targeted treatment to protect your vision. We offer a full spectrum of management options, from specialized eye drops to advanced laser procedures and surgical interventions when necessary. Using state-of-the-art diagnostic equipment, we track even minimal changes in your eye pressure and visual field, allowing us to adjust your treatment plan proactively for the best possible outcomes.  
​  
[See More Details](https://www.eyesurgeonmumbai.com/glaucoma-treatment-mumbai)
* Contact Lenses  
Our contact lens services go beyond simple prescriptions. We offer specialized fitting and consultation for a wide range of contact lenses, including options for complex prescriptions and hard-to-fit eyes. Our experts take time to understand your lifestyle and visual needs, recommending the most appropriate lens type and teaching proper handling and care techniques. We ensure you have both clear vision and optimal comfort with your contact lenses.

[ALL TREATMENTS ](https://www.eyesurgeonmumbai.com/treatments)

![Best Eye Clinic for Kids](https://static.wixstatic.com/media/1231c0_fe479ce6a7c345b385c0f2eba641775b~mv2.webp/v1/fill/w_147,h_84,al_c,q_80,usm_0.66_1.00_0.01,blur_2,enc_avif,quality_auto/kid%201.webp)

### Key Treatments

* Retinal Surgery  
The retina is the light-sensitive layer at the back of your eye that transforms visual information into signals your brain can understand. Our comprehensive retinal care addresses conditions ranging from diabetic retinopathy to retinal detachment. Using our advanced Turbovit system for retinal surgery, we perform precise microsurgical procedures to repair and protect this delicate tissue. Our retinal treatment options include specialized injections for age-related macular degeneration (ARMD), helping preserve vision for patients with this challenging condition. Each treatment plan is carefully tailored to the specific needs of your retinal health.  
​  
[See More Details](https://www.eyesurgeonmumbai.com/retinal-surgery-mumbai)
* Retina Injections  
Age-related macular degeneration can significantly impact your central vision, affecting your ability to read, recognize faces, and perform detailed tasks. Our specialized retinal injection treatments help manage this condition by delivering medication directly to the affected area. These precise injections can help slow disease progression and, in many cases, preserve vital central vision. We use the latest treatment protocols and advanced imaging technology to monitor your response to treatment, adjusting our approach as needed for optimal results.  
​  
[See More Details](https://www.eyesurgeonmumbai.com/retinal-injections-mumbai)
* Pediatric Ophthalmology  
Children's eye care requires special expertise and a gentle touch. Our pediatric ophthalmology services address the unique visual needs of young patients, from routine eye examinations to complex conditions like squint (strabismus). For children with misaligned eyes, our squint surgery services offer precise correction that can improve both vision and appearance. We create a child-friendly environment and use age-appropriate examination techniques to ensure our young patients feel comfortable while receiving expert care.  
​  
[See More Details](https://www.eyesurgeonmumbai.com/pediatric-eye-care-mumbai)
* Dry Eye Clinic  
Chronic dry eye can cause persistent discomfort and affect your quality of life. Our dedicated dry eye clinic offers comprehensive evaluation and treatment of this common condition. We use advanced diagnostic tools to analyze your tear composition and production, allowing us to develop a targeted treatment plan. From specialized eye drops to advanced therapies, we help restore comfort and protect your eye health.  
​  
[See More Details](https://www.eyesurgeonmumbai.com/dry-eye-treatment-mumbai)

[BOOK CONSULTATION ](https://www.eyesurgeonmumbai.com/consult)

### Key Treatments

![Best Eye Hospital in Mumbai](https://static.wixstatic.com/media/1231c0_3bb5169ab02e4aa183abd36447d76060~mv2.webp/v1/fill/w_147,h_84,al_c,q_80,usm_0.66_1.00_0.01,blur_2,enc_avif,quality_auto/eye%201.webp)

* General Ophthalmology  
Our comprehensive eye care services go beyond treating specific conditions. Through thorough eye examinations, we evaluate every aspect of your eye health, from vision testing to pressure checks and retinal examinations. We believe in preventive care and early detection, using advanced diagnostic equipment to identify potential issues before they become serious problems. Our general ophthalmology services provide the foundation for maintaining healthy vision throughout your life, with personalized advice on eye care and protection.
* Oculoplasty & Botox  
The delicate tissues around your eyes deserve specialized care. Our oculoplastic services address both functional and aesthetic concerns, from drooping eyelids that impair vision to tear duct problems that cause constant tearing. We also offer Botox treatments for medical conditions like blepharospasm (involuntary eye twitching) and for cosmetic enhancement. Each procedure is performed with meticulous attention to detail, preserving natural appearance while improving function and comfort.  
​  
[See More Details](https://www.eyesurgeonmumbai.com/oculoplastic-surgery-botox-mumbai)
* ICL  
For patients who may not be candidates for LASIK, ICL offers an excellent alternative for vision correction. These advanced lenses are placed inside the eye, working in harmony with your natural eye structure to provide clear vision. Unlike contact lenses, ICLs require no daily maintenance and are invisible to others. The procedure is reversible and offers UV protection while correcting your vision, making it an attractive option for many patients seeking freedom from glasses.  
​  
[See More Details](https://www.eyesurgeonmumbai.com/icl-surgery-mumbai)
* Cornea Services  
The cornea is your eye's clear front window, crucial for focusing light and protecting deeper eye structures. Our corneal services address conditions ranging from infections to inherited disorders. We offer advanced treatments including corneal transplantation when necessary, using precise microsurgical techniques to restore clarity and vision. Our expertise includes both traditional full-thickness transplants and newer, selective layer replacement procedures for optimal outcomes.  
​  
[See More Details](https://www.eyesurgeonmumbai.com/corneal-transplant-surgery-mumbai)
* Mutlifocal, Trifocal, Toric IOL and EDOF IOL  
Modern lens implant technology offers exciting possibilities for vision correction during cataract surgery. We offer a full range of premium intraocular lenses, each designed to meet specific visual needs. Multifocal and trifocal lenses can reduce dependence on glasses for both distance and near vision. Toric lenses correct astigmatism, while EDOF (Extended Depth of Focus) lenses provide enhanced vision across a range of distances. During your consultation, we'll help you choose the best lens option for your lifestyle and visual goals.

CATARACT SURGERY

Most patients return to their daily activities within 24-48 hours. Our micro-incision technique ensures minimal discomfort and optimal results. Treatment duration: 15-20 minutes per eye. ![Still carrying excess baggage under your eyes ??? Well,  why??? 

Non surgical aesthetics are the future of cosmetology and many facial aesthetics procedures are not done without having to go under the knife 

Similarly , an option for eyebags is the Morpheus8

How does it work ?
1. Microneedling and RF combine to create sub dermal tissue breakdown 
2. This stimulates healing and new collagen formation 
3. New collagen is more elastic and makes the skin firm and younger in appearance 
4. It remodels the skin to a new contour hence no more eye bags 

How is this different from surgical blepharoplasty? 
1. It’s not a surgery 
2. It more natural 
3. No fillers so no filler related problems and bumps 
4. No injections and Botox so no frozen faces , your expressions stay natural 
5. Natural looking appearance unlike a sudden change we se post surgery 
6. Subtlety helps when it’s your face , definitely 

How many sessions ? 
A couple to begin with and then maybe a top up at 9-12 months is good for most cases 

If you want to know more please feel free to ask me about it

![Cataract diagnosed, lens selected … you think you’re good to go ?! But wait what about the lens measurement? Every lens is unique in its number and shape (if toric) 
How is this measured ?
1. Manually on an A scan machine 
2. On a modern machine like a Lenstar , Argos or an IOL master 

The measurements are converted into the right IOL powers using modern day calculations and formulae 

Why is this important to know ? 
This decides the prediction of you achieving clear vision post surgery 
It’s a very important pre operative test

Monofocal IOL : works well for distance 

Trifocal IOL : works well for far near and intermediate but has issues for glare and haloes 

EDOF IOL : works well for far and for intermediate distances and not so well for near so you may need to wear reading glasses sometimes 
No glare and haloes with this one 

All lenses are available as toric options for patients with cylindrical powers

![Post cataract surgery blur making you lose your confidence ? 
It’s most likely a posterior capsular o pacification 
A PCO is a film that forms due to cells migrating behind the lens implant , typically a year or two post surgery 
It’s commoner than you would imagine and yes, annoying too !
A laser procedure will solve the issue instantly , it’s a short one, done in the OPD and has no downtime 

Check with your ophthalmologist and get this sorted 
.
.
(Ophthalmology, yag laser pctomy, posterior capsule opacification , after cataract)

![Last night at the eyeconomics session I spoke about the art of spending 

Here’s a summary of what I covered 

1. Abram Maslow theories of wants and needs 
This is a very popular concept that divides our buys into categories of psychological emotional esteem and self actualisation demands 

2. Spending is an art while investing is a science 
The concept of spending involves thinking with your heart and with your brain as well as

3. As a service industry we doctors need to think about the man hours we need to work to find our purchase 
Each heavy expense means you spend more hours at work so that’s the trade off 

4. Spend on what your want not what your neighbour got 
Avoid comparing and buying just for social signalling 

5. At the end of the day remember to spend more time with those who love you as that’s what really matters finally 

6. Don’t buy to impress others 
It’s not going to work because they aren’t even looking
Everyone’s focused in their own lives so it doesn’t matter to them 

7. Between a big ticket spend like a car or a home , go for a home first
That’s the place you will spend maximum time with those close to your heart and create maximum memories too 

So yes, that is how it panned out 
You can still catch it on YouTube anytime 

Thank you to Dr Partha Biswas  President AIOS for the opportunity 

Thank you Dr Sreeni Edakhlon and Dr Umesh Y 
Course Directors for eyeconomics

![Teaching the younger breed to be financially savvy 

Everyone needs to know the difference between prestige spends and real needs 

It’s ok to splurge sometimes but only if you do it smartly is it sustainable 

Tomorrow you’ll get a better insight into this sensitive topic as I’ll share the podium with some eminent ophthalmologists from across India and speak with a pan India audience about the same

![Glaucoma a silent thief of sight 

Well here’s an insight into a Perimetry test for detection of visual field loss due to the abnormal eye pressures 

It’s a simple test but a tedious one so come prepared and give it your best shot 

To prepare for a perinetry test :

1.Sleep well the night before 
2. Avoid gadget use prior to the test 
3. Schedule it a comfortable time / avoid your nap time as you will be drowsy and the test won’t be accurate 
4. Stay focused and don’t let your thoughts run wild as again you will be distracted and there will be an unreliable result 
5. Focus on the fixation target and remember to blink often while the test is on 

Schedule your test today @isighteyecare 
#glaucoma
#perimetry #mumbai #eyecare

## Contoura LASIK Vision Correction in Mumbai: Advanced Vision Enhancement Technology

![Dr. Nikhil Nasta performing LASIK surgery at I Sight Eye Care Mumbai](https://static.wixstatic.com/media/1231c0_d203a921c568421d9e28b50327e29bd8~mv2.webp/v1/fill/w_147,h_110,al_c,q_80,usm_0.66_1.00_0.01,blur_2,enc_avif,quality_auto/1.webp)

## What is Contoura LASIK?

Contoura Vision is the most advanced FDA-approved topography-guided LASIK technology that provides personalized vision correction. Unlike traditional LASIK, Contoura LASIK creates a detailed topographic mapping of your cornea using over 22,000 unique data points to guide the laser treatment for optimal results.

## Who is a Good Candidate for Lasik?

![Best LASIK treatment in Bandra Mumbai for clear vision without glasses](https://static.wixstatic.com/media/1231c0_710093aacd6247dab25ac19e80ecda48~mv2.jpeg/v1/fill/w_147,h_98,al_c,q_80,usm_0.66_1.00_0.01,blur_2,enc_avif,quality_auto/2.jpeg)

* Adults 18 years or older with stable vision
* Patients with myopia up to -8.00D
* Patients with astigmatism up to -3.00D
* Healthy corneas with adequate thickness
* No active eye diseases or autoimmune conditions

## FREQUENTLY ASKED QUESTIONS (FAQ'S FOR LASIK)

Q1: What is the cost of LASIK surgery in Mumbai?  
A: The average cost of LASIK surgery in Mumbai ranges between ₹35,000 to ₹1,00,000 depending on the technology used, surgeon’s expertise, and clinic facilities.

​

Q2: Is LASIK surgery safe for all patients?  
A: LASIK is safe for most patients, but eligibility depends on corneal thickness, eye health, and stable prescription. A detailed consultation is required.

​

Q3: How long does LASIK surgery take?  
A: The procedure itself takes about 15–20 minutes for both eyes, while the entire visit (prep + recovery) may take 2–3 hours.

​

Q4: How soon can I see after LASIK?  
A: Most patients notice clearer vision within 24 hours. Vision continues to improve over a week with complete stabilization in 1–3 months.

​

Q5: Is LASIK painful?  
A: No, LASIK is painless. Numbing eye drops are used, and patients only feel mild pressure during the procedure.

​

Q6: Can LASIK permanently remove glasses?  
A: Yes, LASIK corrects refractive errors (myopia, hyperopia, astigmatism), reducing or eliminating the need for glasses or contact lenses.

​

Q7: What are the side effects of LASIK surgery?  
A: Temporary dryness, glare, or halos may occur, usually resolving within a few weeks. Rare complications can be minimized with an experienced surgeon.

​

Q8: What is the recovery time after LASIK?  
A: Most patients resume work within 1–2 days, but full healing may take 3 months. Avoid swimming, rubbing eyes, and heavy exercise during early recovery.

​

Q9: Who is not eligible for LASIK surgery?  
A: People with thin corneas, uncontrolled diabetes, autoimmune conditions, or unstable vision prescriptions may not qualify for LASIK.

​

Q10: Why choose Dr. Nikhil Nasta for LASIK in Mumbai?  
A: Dr. Nikhil Nasta is a trusted eye surgeon in Mumbai with expertise in advanced LASIK and Contoura Vision, ensuring safe and precise vision correction.

​

​

Disclaimer: This information is for educational purposes only. Individual cases vary; consult a specialist for personalized advice.

## FREQUENTLY ASKED QUESTIONS FOR CATARACT

* When should cataract surgery be done?  
When cloudy vision affects reading, driving, glare, or daily tasks and glasses no longer help surgery offers the best, lasting solution.
* Is surgery painful and how long does it take?  
With numbing drops, patients feel no pain. Phacoemulsification through a micro‑incision typically takes 10–20 minutes per eye.
* What are premium IOL options?  
Monofocal (single distance), toric (astigmatism correction), multifocal/trifocal (distance‑intermediate‑near), and EDOF lenses for a broader range of focus.
* Will I need glasses after surgery?  
With monofocal IOLs, readers are usually needed. Trifocal/EDOF lenses reduce dependence across distances; results vary by eye health and expectations.
* Can both eyes be operated on the same day?  
Many prefer staged surgery a few days apart; same‑day bilateral is considered case‑by‑case after discussing safety and logistics.
* How soon can I resume normal activities?  
Most resume light work in 2–3 days. Avoid rubbing, dusty environments, heavy lifting, and swimming for the period your surgeon advises.
* What about glare/halos with premium lenses?  
Some patients notice night halos early; these typically lessen as the brain adapts. Proper lens selection minimizes unwanted effects.
* Is cataract surgery safe for diabetics?  
Yes, with optimized sugar control and careful retina evaluation. We coordinate with your physician and monitor macular health closely.
* What tests are done before surgery?  
Biometry, corneal curvature/astigmatism mapping, macular scan if needed, tear film assessment, and general medical fitness checks.
* Why choose I Sight Eye Care for cataract?  
Experienced surgical team, precise biometry, premium lens counseling, and thorough follow‑up at Khar & Dadar clinics.

## FREQUENTLY ASKED QUESTIONS FOR RETINAL SURGERY

* When is retinal surgery needed?  
For retinal detachment, macular holes, epiretinal membranes, diabetic retinopathy complications, or vitreous hemorrhage that threaten sight.
* What are the main retinal surgical procedures?  
Vitrectomy, scleral buckle, pneumatic retinopexy, membrane peel, and endolaser photocoagulation are commonly performed.
* Is retinal surgery urgent?  
Yes, conditions like retinal detachment are surgical emergencies; early treatment is crucial to preserve vision.
* How long is recovery after vitrectomy?  
Initial recovery is 2–4 weeks; final vision may take months to stabilize, depending on the condition treated.
* Do I need to position face-down after surgery?  
For macular hole or certain detachments with gas tamponade, face-down positioning may be required for 1–2 weeks.
* Are there risks with retinal surgery?  
Risks include cataract progression, infection, bleeding, pressure changes, or recurrence of detachment. Modern techniques minimize complications.
* Will I regain full vision after retinal surgery?  
Outcomes depend on disease severity and how quickly surgery is done. Earlier intervention usually means better results.
* Is retinal surgery painful?  
No. Anesthesia (local or general) ensures you’re comfortable. Some soreness or mild irritation is expected after.
* Can diabetes affect retinal surgery outcomes?  
Yes. Uncontrolled diabetes can cause recurrent bleeding or swelling. Sugar control and follow-up are vital for success.
* Why choose I Sight Eye Care for retinal surgery?  
Expertise in vitreoretinal techniques, advanced diagnostics (OCT, fundus imaging), and personalized care at Khar & Dadar.

Disclaimer: This information is for educational purposes only. Individual cases vary; consult a specialist for personalized advice.

## FREQUENTLY ASKED QUESTIONS ABOUT OCULOPLASTIC SURGERY AND BOTOX

* What is oculoplastic surgery?  
It is specialized plastic surgery around the eyes, treating droopy eyelids (ptosis), eye bags, tumors, injuries, and cosmetic issues.
* What cosmetic concerns can Botox treat?  
Botox reduces fine lines, crow’s feet, frown lines, forehead wrinkles, and helps correct eyelid spasms.
* Is oculoplastic surgery only cosmetic?  
No. It also corrects functional problems like blocked tear ducts, eyelid malpositions, and orbital diseases.
* How long do Botox results last?  
Typically 3–6 months, after which repeat treatment maintains results.
* Does oculoplastic surgery leave scars?  
Most incisions are hidden in natural creases; scars are minimal and fade with time.
* Is Botox safe near the eyes?  
Yes, when administered by an experienced oculoplastic surgeon. It is FDA-approved and safe in expert hands.
* What is the recovery time for eyelid surgery?  
Mild swelling and bruising resolve in 1–2 weeks; full results are seen in 1–3 months.
* Does oculoplastic surgery improve vision?  
Yes, lifting droopy eyelids or removing large bags can improve field of vision along with cosmetic enhancement.
* Are results from surgery permanent?  
Functional corrections are permanent; cosmetic improvements last years but natural aging continues.
* Why choose Dr. Nikhil Nasta for oculoplastic and Botox?  
Dual expertise in functional ophthalmology and cosmetic enhancements, with advanced techniques at Khar & Dadar.

Disclaimer: This information is for educational purposes only. Individual cases vary; consult a specialist for personalized advice.

## Advanced Corneal Transplant Surgery

At I-Sight Eye Care and Surgery, we offer state-of-the-art corneal transplant procedures using the latest surgical techniques. Our experienced team specializes in all types of corneal transplantation, providing personalized care for optimal vision restoration.

![Advanced corneal transplant surgery at eye clinic in Dadar and Khar](https://static.wixstatic.com/media/1231c0_5b6b39fcbd454a6c80e7ef32a4ee4af4~mv2.webp/v1/fill/w_147,h_74,al_c,q_80,usm_0.66_1.00_0.01,blur_2,enc_avif,quality_auto/3.webp)

## Types of Corneal Transplants We Offer

### Full Thickness Corneal Transplant (PK)

* Complete cornea replacement
* Traditional transplant method
* Suitable for severe corneal damage
* Full-thickness donor tissue

### Partial Thickness Corneal Transplant (DALK)

* Front and middle cornea layers replacement
* Preserves inner corneal layer
* Reduced rejection risk
* Faster recovery time

### Endothelial Keratoplasty (DMEK/DSAEK)

* Inner layer replacement only
* Minimally invasive
* Faster visual recovery
* Lower rejection rates
* Smaller incision size

# Corneal Transplant Surgery in Mumbai – Restoring Vision with Keratoplasty

![Successful corneal transplant patient at leading eye hospital in Khar and Dadar Mumbai](https://static.wixstatic.com/media/1231c0_98ec89198ec8427db7938581a19f57bb~mv2.webp/v1/fill/w_147,h_98,al_c,q_80,usm_0.66_1.00_0.01,blur_2,enc_avif,quality_auto/IMG_0250.webp)

## FREQUENTLY ASKED QUESTIONS ABOUT CORNEAL TRANSPLANT SURGERY

* What is corneal transplant surgery?  
Replacement of the damaged cornea with healthy donor tissue (keratoplasty).
* Who needs corneal transplantation?  
Patients with keratoconus, corneal scarring, infections, thinning, degeneration, or trauma.
* Are there different types of corneal transplants?  
Yes – penetrating keratoplasty (full thickness), lamellar keratoplasty (partial thickness), and endothelial keratoplasty (DSEK/DMEK).
* How long is recovery?  
Initial recovery takes weeks, full stabilization may take 6–12 months.
* Is corneal transplant safe?  
Yes, modern surgical techniques have high success rates, though rejection and infection risks exist.
* Can corneal transplant restore 20/20 vision?  
Many patients regain excellent vision, but outcomes depend on underlying disease and healing.
* How to know if my body rejects the graft?  
Redness, pain, sensitivity to light, or sudden vision drop are warning signs – immediate medical care is needed.
* What precautions are required after transplant?  
Regular eye drops, follow-up visits, avoiding trauma, and wearing protective glasses.
* How long does a corneal graft last?  
On average 10–15 years, though many last much longer with good care.
* Why choose I Sight Eye Care?  
Access to donor tissue, advanced surgical microscopes, and expert post-op care at Khar & Dadar.

## Understanding Squint (Strabismus)

![Best eye specialist in Mumbai for squint correction and strabismus surgery](https://static.wixstatic.com/media/1231c0_0a9fd968938e4ac7880fa133a08b7e24~mv2.png/v1/fill/w_75,h_75,al_c,q_85,usm_0.66_1.00_0.01,blur_2,enc_avif,quality_auto/6.png)

Squint is a condition where the eyes are misaligned, with one eye turning inward, outward, upward, or downward. Types include:

* Esotropia (inward turning)
* Exotropia (outward turning)
* Hypertropia (upward turning)
* Hypotropia (downward turning)

## Who Needs Squint Surgery?

![Dr. Nikhil Nasta performing squint eye surgery at I Sight Eye Care Khar Mumbai](https://static.wixstatic.com/media/1231c0_0abdea7c4052492788c76d3e72b94010~mv2.png/v1/crop/x_0,y_81,w_379,h_284/fill/w_95,h_71,al_c,q_85,usm_0.66_1.00_0.01,blur_2,enc_avif,quality_auto/2.png)

Squint correction may be recommended for:

* Children with persistent eye misalignment
* Adults with long-standing squint
* Patients with double vision
* Those with head-turn positions
* Cases unresponsive to non-surgical treatment

## FREQUENTLY ASKED QUESTIONS ABOUT SQUINT CORRECTION SURGERY

* What is squint surgery?  
A procedure to realign the eye muscles to correct strabismus (misaligned eyes).
* Is squint surgery only cosmetic?  
No. It improves binocular vision, depth perception, and eye coordination in addition to appearance.
* At what age should squint be treated?  
Early treatment (childhood) gives best results, but adults can also benefit.
* How long does squint surgery take?  
Usually 45–90 minutes, often under general anesthesia for children.
* Is hospitalization required?  
No, most are daycare procedures with same-day discharge.
* What is the recovery period?  
Redness and mild discomfort last 1–2 weeks; alignment improves within days.
* Can squint recur after surgery?  
Yes, in some cases especially if underlying issues persist. Regular follow-up reduces risk.
* Will glasses still be needed?  
Sometimes yes – glasses or vision therapy may still be required depending on refractive error.
* Is squint surgery painful?  
No. Anesthesia ensures comfort. Mild soreness or gritty feeling resolves quickly.
* Why choose I Sight Eye Care?  
Expert strabismus management for children and adults with advanced surgical techniques at Khar & Dadar.

## ICL (Implantable Contact Lens) Surgery

![Ophthalmologist in Mumbai explaining ICL surgery as an alternative to LASIK for vision correction](https://static.wixstatic.com/media/1231c0_3b9a7f081026480bac2de487a8b75f27~mv2.png/v1/crop/x_0,y_704,w_1092,h_403/fill/w_49,h_18,al_c,q_85,usm_0.66_1.00_0.01,blur_2,enc_avif,quality_auto/ICL.png)

## What is ICL Surgery?

![Implantable Contact Lens (ICL) surgery illustration showing lens placement inside the eye at I Sight Eye Care Mumbai](https://static.wixstatic.com/media/1231c0_7a36910aebac4e68abf565da8f48be88~mv2.jpeg/v1/fill/w_75,h_70,al_c,q_80,usm_0.66_1.00_0.01,blur_2,enc_avif,quality_auto/3.jpeg)

ICL (Implantable Collamer Lens) surgery involves placing a specialized lens inside the eye to correct vision problems. Unlike LASIK, which reshapes the cornea, ICL adds a new lens while preserving the eye's natural structure.

## Ideal Candidates for ICL

ICL surgery is perfect for:

* High myopia (nearsightedness) patients
* High hyperopia (farsightedness) patients
* Patients with thin corneas
* Those unsuitable for LASIK

# ICL Surgery in Mumbai (Phakic IOL for High Myopia)

![IMG_9627.webp](https://static.wixstatic.com/media/1231c0_da6c83b50c2a4e63a45106a090ee825b~mv2.webp/v1/fill/w_147,h_117,al_c,q_80,usm_0.66_1.00_0.01,blur_2,enc_avif,quality_auto/IMG_9627.webp)

Permanent contact lenses you never have to remove, giving clarity that stays with you.

## FREQUENTLY ASKED QUESTIONS FOR ICL

* Who is ideal for ICL instead of LASIK?  
People with high myopia/astigmatism, thin or irregular corneas, or dry eye who want quick recovery and crisp optics without corneal reshaping.
* Is the ICL visible or felt?  
No. The lens sits behind the iris and in front of your natural lens—undetectable to others and not felt by you.
* Is ICL reversible?  
Yes. The lens can be removed or exchanged if future needs change (e.g., cataract surgery later in life).
* Can ICL correct astigmatism?  
Yes—Toric ICL models correct significant astigmatism alongside myopia for sharper vision.
* How long does the procedure and recovery take?  
Surgery takes \~15–20 minutes per eye. Most patients see well within 24–48 hours with minimal activity restrictions.
* Is ICL safe for dry‑eye patients?  
Often yes. Because the cornea isn’t ablated, ICL tends to be friendlier for people prone to dry eye.
* What tests are required before ICL?  
We measure anterior chamber depth, white‑to‑white, corneal health, pupil size and calculate lens size/power precisely.
* Will I need glasses after ICL?  
Most daily activities are glasses‑free. Tiny residual power, if present, can be corrected with light specs or a touch‑up plan.
* What are potential side effects?  
Early halos/glare, temporary pressure rise, or inflammation are monitored and managed; regular follow‑ups keep the eye safe long‑term.
* Why I Sight Eye Care for ICL?  
Accurate sizing protocols, toric planning, and careful postoperative monitoring at Khar & Dadar ensure crisp visual outcomes.

## Understanding ARMD

![retinal injections for ARMD in Mumbai](https://static.wixstatic.com/media/1231c0_3d91a2911fc3441a898d0b2a92bed995~mv2.jpg/v1/fill/w_147,h_131,al_c,q_80,usm_0.66_1.00_0.01,blur_2,enc_avif,quality_auto/2.jpg)

Age-Related Macular Degeneration affects the macula, the central part of the retina responsible for detailed vision. We treat both types:

### Dry ARMD

* More common form (85-90%)
* Gradual vision loss
* Preventive treatment approach
* Regular monitoring required

### Wet ARMD

* Less common but more severe
* Rapid vision loss possible
* Requires immediate treatment
* Responsive to injections

# Retinal Injections in Mumbai (Anti-VEGF for ARMD & Retinal Diseases)

## FREQUENTLY ASKED QUESTIONS FOR RETINAL INJECTIONS

* What are retinal injections used for?  
Mainly for wet age-related macular degeneration (ARMD), diabetic macular edema, and retinal vein occlusion swelling.
* What medicines are used in injections?  
Anti-VEGF agents like Ranibizumab, Aflibercept, Bevacizumab, and steroids for certain cases.
* Are retinal injections painful?  
No. The eye is numbed with anesthetic drops. Patients may feel mild pressure or scratchy sensation briefly.
* How often are injections required?  
Depends on disease. Initially monthly, then spaced out with “treat-and-extend” protocols as the retina stabilizes.
* How long do injections take?  
Just a few minutes. Most patients are in and out of the clinic within 30 minutes.
* What are the side effects?  
Mild redness or floaters may occur. Rare risks include infection, bleeding, or retinal detachment.
* Will injections cure ARMD?  
No cure exists, but injections control abnormal blood vessel growth and preserve vision long-term if maintained.
* What happens if I skip an injection?  
Missing doses can allow disease to reactivate, causing sudden vision drop. Consistent treatment is critical.
* Is there a difference between branded and biosimilar injections?  
Both can be effective; choice depends on clinical need, safety, and affordability.
* Why I Sight Eye Care for injections?  
Expert retina team, sterile protocols, and patient-centric scheduling at Khar & Dadar for safe ongoing care.

Disclaimer: This information is for educational purposes only. Individual cases vary; consult a specialist for personalized advice.

## Comprehensive Glaucoma Management and Treatment

At I-Sight Eye Care and Surgery, we offer state-of-the-art glaucoma diagnosis, management, and treatment services. Our expert team uses advanced technology to detect glaucoma early and provide personalized treatment plans to preserve your vision.

![Visual field test for early glaucoma detection at Dr. Nikhil Nasta’s I Sight Eye Care Mumbai](https://static.wixstatic.com/media/1231c0_b04a3aaa8ed0426d97c68abf3c2ea9dd~mv2.webp/v1/fill/w_147,h_77,al_c,q_80,usm_0.66_1.00_0.01,blur_2,enc_avif,quality_auto/5.webp)

## Understanding Glaucoma

![Diagram showing optic nerve damage caused by glaucoma at I Sight Eye Care Mumbai](https://static.wixstatic.com/media/1231c0_993e0052797c46c58e0f5c32451c1b8e~mv2.jpg/v1/fill/w_126,h_126,al_c,q_80,usm_0.66_1.00_0.01,blur_2,enc_avif,quality_auto/eye-anatomy-of-glaucoma.jpg)

Glaucoma is a group of eye conditions that damage the optic nerve, often due to high eye pressure. We specialize in managing all types:

* Open-Angle Glaucoma
* Angle-Closure Glaucoma
* Normal-Tension Glaucoma
* Secondary Glaucoma
* Congenital Glaucoma

## Advanced Diagnostic Technology

Our facility features:

* OCT (Optical Coherence Tomography)
* Visual Field Testing
* Pachymetry - Corneal Thickness Measurement
* Gonioscopy
* IOP Measurement
* Nerve Fiber Analysis
* Tracking Progression by serial RNFL Pictures

![Glaucoma diagnosis with advanced eye pressure testing equipment at I Sight Eye Care Khar-Bandra and Dadar](https://static.wixstatic.com/media/1231c0_2f73538b3c754df086ab163235754c01~mv2.jpg/v1/fill/w_147,h_98,al_c,q_80,usm_0.66_1.00_0.01,blur_2,enc_avif,quality_auto/3.jpg)

## FREQUENTLY ASKED QUESTIONS ABOUT GLAUCOMA

* What is glaucoma?  
A group of diseases causing optic nerve damage, often due to high eye pressure, leading to gradual irreversible vision loss if untreated.
* What are the symptoms?  
Most types are silent until advanced. Some acute cases cause sudden pain, halos, redness, or blurred vision.
* How is glaucoma diagnosed?  
Through eye pressure check, optic nerve imaging, OCT, visual field tests, gonioscopy, and corneal thickness measurements.
* What treatments are available?  
Eye drops, oral medicines, laser trabeculoplasty, and surgeries like trabeculectomy or drainage implants.
* Can glaucoma be cured?  
No, but it can be controlled to prevent vision loss. Early detection and treatment are key.
* How often should I get checked for glaucoma?  
Every 1–2 years after age 40, or earlier/more often if you have family history, diabetes, or high eye pressure.
* What lifestyle tips help glaucoma?  
Regular exercise, healthy diet, controlling blood pressure/diabetes, avoiding smoking, and adhering to prescribed drops.
* Is glaucoma hereditary?  
Yes, family history significantly increases risk. Screening relatives is important.
* What happens if I stop using drops?  
Eye pressure rises again, risking faster nerve damage. Compliance is crucial.
* Why I Sight Eye Care for glaucoma management?  
Full diagnostics, tailored therapy, advanced lasers and surgical backup at Khar & Dadar.

## Common Symptoms

![Child eye specialist in Mumbai explaining treatment options to parents at Khar-Bandra clinic](https://static.wixstatic.com/media/1231c0_f94c41d0cb394d53853a3169638dfb4a~mv2.jpg/v1/fill/w_147,h_98,al_c,q_80,usm_0.66_1.00_0.01,blur_2,enc_avif,quality_auto/3.jpg)

* Strabismus (Eye Misalignment) : Using advanced diagnostic techniques, we evaluate and treat all forms of strabismus, offering both non-surgical and surgical solutions when necessary.
* Refractive Errors : We provide precise vision correction for nearsightedness, farsightedness, and astigmatism, with a focus on the unique needs of growing children.

## Myopia in Children

![Pediatric myopia and squint treatment for children at Dr. Nikhil Nasta’s eye clinic in Mumbai](https://static.wixstatic.com/media/11062b_957e79ea0e654e27a1d85d0c295f8fe0~mv2.jpg/v1/fill/w_147,h_98,al_c,q_80,usm_0.66_1.00_0.01,blur_2,enc_avif,quality_auto/Small%20Child%20with%20Large%20Glasses.jpg)

* Myopia, or nearsightedness, is becoming increasingly common in kids due to more screen time and less outdoor activity. Children with myopia see nearby objects clearly but struggle with distant ones, like the classroom board.
* Early signs: squinting, sitting too close to screens, frequent eye rubbing, or headaches.
* Management: Glasses, special myopia-control lenses, low-dose eye drops, and healthy habits like outdoor play. Regular eye check-ups help slow progression and protect long-term vision.

## FREQUENTLY ASKED QUESTIONS ABOUT PEDIATRIC EYE CARE

* When should a child have their first eye exam?  
Ideally at 6 months, 3 years, and before school entry, or earlier if vision issues are suspected.
* What eye conditions are common in children?  
Squint (strabismus), lazy eye (amblyopia), refractive errors (glasses), pediatric cataracts, and blocked tear ducts.
* How do I know if my child needs glasses?  
Signs include squinting, sitting too close to screens, frequent rubbing, headaches, and poor school performance.
* What is lazy eye in children?  
Amblyopia is when one eye has reduced vision because the brain favors the other eye. Early treatment prevents permanent vision loss.
* Is squint surgery safe for children?  
Yes, squint correction is safe and often done under general anesthesia to restore alignment and improve vision.
* How is pediatric cataract treated?  
Surgery with lens implantation is performed early to prevent vision loss and amblyopia.
* Can children wear contact lenses?  
Yes, under proper supervision, children can safely use contact lenses for sports or high prescriptions.
* Does screen time affect children’s eyes?  
Excessive screen use can cause digital eye strain, dryness, and worsen myopia (nearsightedness).
* How to prevent myopia in children?  
Outdoor play, limiting screen time, balanced nutrition, and regular eye exams.
* Why choose Dr. Nikhil Nasta for pediatric eye care?  
Expert in diagnosing and treating childhood eye disorders with a child-friendly approach at Khar & Dadar clinics.

Disclaimer: This information is for educational purposes only. Individual cases vary; consult a specialist for personalized advice.

## Understanding Dry Eye Disease

![Best treatment for dry eyes and eye irritation in Mumbai](https://static.wixstatic.com/media/1231c0_55b65633c0894911b86b518690f9207c~mv2.jpg/v1/fill/w_147,h_98,al_c,q_80,usm_0.66_1.00_0.01,blur_2,enc_avif,quality_auto/3.jpg)

Dry eye is a chronic condition affecting tear production and quality. We treat various types:

* Aqueous Deficient Dry Eye
* Evaporative Dry Eye
* Mixed Type Dry Eye
* Meibomian Gland Dysfunction
* Contact Lens-Related Dry Eye

## Common Symptoms

![Specialist eye clinic in Mumbai for dry eye disease therapy and management](https://static.wixstatic.com/media/1231c0_746a11070d1140dab119ffbb3cd0ef06~mv2.webp/v1/fill/w_147,h_98,al_c,q_80,usm_0.66_1.00_0.01,blur_2,enc_avif,quality_auto/4.webp)

* Eye irritation and burning
* Grittiness or foreign body sensation
* Blurred or fluctuating vision
* Light sensitivity
* Eye fatigue
* Excessive tearing
* Redness

## FREQUENTLY ASKED QUESTIONS ABOUT DRY EYE THERAPY

* What is dry eye disease?  
Dry eye occurs when the eyes don’t produce enough tears or when tears evaporate too quickly, causing irritation, redness, and blurry vision.
* What are the symptoms of dry eye?  
Common signs include burning, stinging, gritty sensation, watery eyes, light sensitivity, and difficulty with screen use.
* What causes dry eye?  
Aging, excessive screen time, contact lenses, LASIK history, hormonal changes, certain medications, and autoimmune diseases.
* How is dry eye diagnosed?  
Eye specialists use tests like Schirmer’s test, tear breakup time, and meibomian gland analysis to confirm diagnosis.
* What treatments are available for dry eye in Mumbai?  
Artificial tears, lubricating gels, punctal plugs, anti-inflammatory eye drops, and advanced therapies like IPL or LipiFlow.
* Is dry eye permanent?  
It can be chronic, but with proper treatment symptoms can be controlled and quality of life improved.
* Can lifestyle changes help dry eye?  
Yes – reducing screen time, using humidifiers, blinking exercises, omega-3 supplements, and staying hydrated.
* Does LASIK cause dry eye?  
Yes, temporary dry eye is common after LASIK, but symptoms usually improve with time and treatment.
* What happens if dry eye is left untreated?  
It may lead to eye infections, corneal damage, and reduced vision quality.
* Why choose Dr. Nikhil Nasta for dry eye treatment?  
Specialized diagnostic tools, advanced therapies, and personalized care at Khar & Dadar clinics.

Disclaimer: This information is for educational purposes only. Individual cases vary; consult a specialist for personalized advice.

## Understanding Multifocal IOLs

![Best multifocal IOL implant specialist in Mumbai for cataract surgery](https://static.wixstatic.com/media/1231c0_3e73e3d0a4a34296a11744e8c73fa280~mv2.jpg/v1/fill/w_147,h_105,al_c,q_80,usm_0.66_1.00_0.01,blur_2,enc_avif,quality_auto/1.jpg)

Multifocal IOLs are advanced artificial lenses that provide clear vision at multiple distances:

* Distance vision (driving, watching TV)
* Intermediate vision (computer work)
* Near vision (reading, mobile phones)
* Reduced dependence on glasses
* Enhanced quality of life

## Comprehensive Treatment Options

### Bifocal IOLs

* Clear vision at two focal points
* Excellent for distance and reading
* High patient satisfaction
* Proven track record

### Trifocal IOLs

* Three distinct focal points
* Superior intermediate vision
* Enhanced range of vision
* Latest technology

### Extended Depth of Focus (EDOF) IOLs

* Continuous range of vision
* Natural vision quality
* Reduced glare and halos
* Excellent night vision
* May stilll need glasses for very fine prints
* Almost 0 dependency for day to day use.

# FREQUENTLY ASKED QUESTIONS ABOUT MULTIFOCAL IOL SURGERY  

* What is a Multifocal IOL?  
A Multifocal IOL (intraocular lens) is a premium lens implant used during cataract surgery that provides clear vision for near, intermediate, and distance.
* Who is a good candidate for Multifocal IOL surgery?  
People undergoing cataract surgery who want to reduce dependency on glasses for both reading and distance tasks.
* What are the benefits of Multifocal IOLs?  
They correct vision at multiple distances, reduce or eliminate the need for glasses, and improve quality of life.
* Are there side effects with Multifocal IOLs?  
Some patients may notice halos or glare at night, but these usually adapt over time.
* How long does Multifocal IOL surgery take?  
It takes about 20–30 minutes, performed as a day-care procedure.
* How long do Multifocal IOLs last?  
They are permanent implants designed to last a lifetime.
* Is the surgery painful?  
No, the procedure is painless and done under topical or local anesthesia.
* How soon can I return to normal activities?  
Most patients resume daily activities within 1–2 days. Complete recovery takes 3–4 weeks.
* What is the cost of Multifocal IOL surgery in Mumbai?  
The cost depends on the type of premium lens but typically ranges from ₹60,000–₹1,20,000 per eye.
* Why choose Dr. Nikhil Nasta?  
Expert in premium IOL cataract surgery with advanced equipment and personalized care at Khar & Dadar clinics.

Disclaimer: This information is for educational purposes only. Individual cases vary; consult a specialist for personalized advice.

## Understanding Trifocal IOLs

![Best trifocal IOL treatment for cataract patients in Mumbai](https://static.wixstatic.com/media/1231c0_4de2efbfe7704af092142126e50ba564~mv2.jpg/v1/fill/w_147,h_105,al_c,q_80,usm_0.66_1.00_0.01,blur_2,enc_avif,quality_auto/2.jpg)

Trifocal IOLs represent the latest evolution in lens implant technology, offering:

* Clear vision at three distinct distances
* Seamless transition between focal points
* Superior intermediate vision
* Enhanced visual quality
* Reduced dependence on glasses

## Advantages Over Other IOLs

### Compared to Standard IOLs

* Multiple focal points vs. single focus
* Reduced need for glasses
* Better overall vision quality
* Enhanced lifestyle benefits
* Greater independence

### Compared to Bifocal IOLs

* Added intermediate vision
* Better computer work vision
* More natural vision feeling
* Smoother transitions
* Enhanced clarity

## Key Benefits of Trifocal IOLs

![Clear vision after cataract surgery with trifocal intraocular lens in Mumbai](https://static.wixstatic.com/media/1231c0_ba80646d8f2841c9a1658bff0db03eb2~mv2.jpg/v1/fill/w_147,h_98,al_c,q_80,usm_0.66_1.00_0.01,blur_2,enc_avif,quality_auto/1.jpg)

Modern trifocal implants provide:

* Clear distance vision (driving, TV)
* Sharp intermediate vision (computer work)
* Excellent near vision (reading, phones)
* Natural vision quality
* Night vision capability
* Reduced glare
* Long-term results

## FREQUENTLY ASKED QUESTIONS ABOUT TRIFOCAL IOL SURGERY

1. What is a Trifocal IOL?  
A Trifocal IOL is a premium intraocular lens that corrects vision for near, intermediate, and distance tasks seamlessly.
2. How is a Trifocal IOL different from Multifocal IOL?  
While multifocal lenses provide two ranges (near + distance), trifocal lenses add intermediate range for better digital/computer work.
3. Who should consider Trifocal IOLs?  
Cataract patients who want the highest freedom from glasses, especially professionals using computers extensively.
4. Are there disadvantages to Trifocal IOLs?  
Some may notice mild halos or glare initially, which reduce with adaptation.
5. How long does Trifocal IOL surgery take?  
Around 20–30 minutes per eye as a day-care surgery.
6. Is Trifocal IOL surgery safe?  
Yes, it’s a proven and safe procedure when performed by an experienced surgeon.
7. What is the recovery time?  
Most patients resume work in 2–3 days, with complete recovery in a few weeks.
8. How much does Trifocal IOL surgery cost in Mumbai?  
Typically ranges ₹80,000–₹1,50,000 per eye depending on the lens brand.
9. Can Trifocal IOLs be implanted in both eyes?  
Yes, usually each eye is done a few days apart for safety.
10. Why choose Dr. Nikhil Nasta?  
Renowned cataract surgeon in Mumbai with advanced premium IOL expertise.

# Frequently Asked Questions About Extended Depth of Focus (EDOF) IOL Surgery 

* What is an EDOF IOL?  
An Extended Depth of Focus (EDOF) lens is an advanced cataract lens implant that provides a continuous range of vision, especially sharp distance and intermediate.
* How does EDOF differ from multifocal lenses?  
EDOF lenses stretch the focal range instead of splitting light like multifocals, which means less glare and halos at night.
* Who is suitable for EDOF lenses?  
Patients who want spectacle independence for distance and computer work, and reduced glare, but don’t mind occasional reading glasses.
* What are the benefits of EDOF IOLs?  
Natural vision quality, reduced glare, excellent intermediate vision for computers, laptops, and dashboards.
* Are EDOF IOLs safe?  
Yes, EDOF IOLs are FDA-approved and safe when implanted during cataract surgery.
* Do EDOF lenses remove the need for glasses?  
They greatly reduce dependence, though some patients may still need glasses for very fine near work.
* What is the cost of EDOF IOL surgery in Mumbai?  
Typically ₹70,000–₹1,60,000 per eye depending on brand and hospital facilities.
* Do EDOF lenses cause night glare?  
Much less than multifocals; they are specifically designed to minimize halos.
* How long is recovery after EDOF surgery?  
Most patients see well in 2–3 days, with full visual recovery in a few weeks.
* Why choose Dr. Nikhil Nasta for EDOF IOLs?  
He offers the latest premium IOL technologies with precision surgery at Khar & Dadar clinics.

## Common Reasons People Book an Eye Consultation

Blurry or Fluctuating Vision

Sudden or gradual blurring can be caused by refractive errors, cataracts, or corneal changes. A full diagnostic scan can pinpoint the exact cause.

Digital Eye Strain & Dryness

Mumbai’s long screen hours and air-conditioning cause evaporative dry eye. We offer IPL (Intense Pulsed Light) and Morpheus Radiofrequency therapies that treat the root cause, the meibomian glands.

LASIK / Laser Vision Correction

If you’re tired of glasses or contact lenses, we perform detailed corneal mapping, tear evaluation, and refraction tests to determine which laser technique (SMILE, Contoura, PRK, LASIK) best suits your eyes.

Cataract Evaluation

Early cataracts often go unnoticed until glare and reduced night vision set in. A quick slit-lamp and lens density test can detect them early, before vision loss affects your lifestyle.

Routine Eye Health Check-Up

Even if your vision seems fine, a yearly eye exam helps detect glaucoma, diabetic retinopathy, or early macular degeneration conditions that progress silently without pain.

I-Sight Eyecare and Surgery is a chain of multi-speciality eye care centers, the concept of which was developed by Dr. Nikhil Nasta.

The centers are in two prime Mumbai locations, Khar and Dadar. The facilities are equipped with the latest ophthalmic instruments and operating facilities.

The aim of I-Sight is to provide quality eye care for all patients at affordable prices

Dr. Nikhil Nasta is the founder of I-Sight Eyecare and Surgery, and has 15 years of experience with expertise in ophthalmology surgery. He established the centre to offer a range of skilled ophthalmology services to the people.

He has an M.S. in Ophthalmology from J.N. Medical College, Belgaum (2004), and is a Diplomate of the National Board (D.N.B.). Dr. Nasta also has an International Council of Ophthalmology certification from Cambridge, UK. 

He has completed a Glaucoma short term fellowship, and a Lasers in Diabetic Retinopathy short term fellowship, both at Aravind Eye Hospital, Madurai. He also holds an M.B.B.S. from Padmashree Dr. D.Y.Patil Medical College, Nerul, Navi Mumbai (1999). Dr. Nasta has been awarded a gold medal, the Pfizer Gold Medallion and Plaque, a special certificate for standing 4th in Mumbai University, the Dr. Govind Vishnu Juvekar Prize and the Smt. Chandanmohan Gold Medal.

He has experience in cataract extraction, glaucoma surgeries, refractive procedures, squint surgeries, oculoplastic procedures and corneal treatments. He is considered one of the best LASIK surgery doctors in Mumbai.

### Dr. Nikhil Nasta – An Award-Winning Ophthalmologist in Mumbai

Dr. Nikhil Nasta, founder of I Sight Eyecare and Surgery (Khar & Dadar), has been consistently recognized for his excellence in ophthalmology, cataract surgery, LASIK, and robotic eye procedures. Over the years, his dedication to precise, ethical, and patient-centric eye care has earned him numerous accolades from leading national and international medical associations.

Some of his recent honours include recognition from the Bombay Ophthalmologists’ Association (BOA), awards for excellence in refractive and cataract surgery, and commendations for community initiatives promoting preventive eye health and early glaucoma detection.

At I Sight Eyecare, Dr. Nasta combines advanced technology with compassionate care—ensuring that every patient receives clear, comfortable vision through minimally invasive treatments such as Contoura LASIK, Morpheus eye rejuvenation, and dry-eye therapy.

These awards stand as a testament to his belief that modern technology and personalized attention go hand in hand in restoring sight and improving lives.

If you’re looking for an award-winning eye specialist in Mumbai, book a consultation at I Sight Eyecare and Surgery to experience trusted expertise and lasting vision clarity.

## What Is a Cataract?

A cataract is the natural clouding of the eye’s lens. The lens, which is normally clear, becomes opaque over time due to aging, diabetes, steroid use, injury, or genetics.

Symptoms include:

* Blurred or foggy vision
* Glare or halos around lights
* Difficulty driving at night
* Frequent changes in glasses power
* Washed-out colors

Cataracts do not improve with medicines or eye drops. The only effective treatment is surgery.   

For patients unsure whether their symptoms are cataract or something else, a complete evaluation is available here:<https://www.eyesurgeonmumbai.com/consult>   

## When Should Cataract Surgery Be Done?

Modern cataract surgery is no longer delayed until vision becomes extremely poor.

You should consider surgery when:

* Vision interferes with daily activities
* You struggle with reading or mobile screens
* Driving at night feels unsafe
* Your glasses no longer help

Delaying surgery unnecessarily can make the cataract harder and slightly increase surgical complexity.   

## Types of Cataract Surgery in Mumbai   

### 1\. Phacoemulsification (Micro Incision Surgery)

The most common and advanced technique. A tiny incision is made, the cataract is emulsified using ultrasound, and replaced with a foldable lens.

Benefits:

* No stitches
* Quick recovery
* Minimal discomfort
* Day-care procedure

### 2\. Laser-Assisted Cataract Surgery

Femtosecond laser improves precision in certain cases.   

### 3\. Premium IOL Cataract Surgery

We offer:

* Trifocal lenses

## Frequently Asked Questions (People Also Ask)

### 1\. Is cataract surgery painful?

No. It is performed under local anesthesia. You may feel mild pressure but no pain.

### 2\. How long does cataract surgery take?

Usually 10–20 minutes per eye.

### 3\. Can cataract come back after surgery?

No. Once removed, it does not return. Some patients may develop posterior capsular opacification, which is easily treated with laser.

### 4\. What is the best age for cataract surgery?

There is no fixed age. Surgery is done when vision affects daily life.

### 5\. Can both eyes be operated together?

Usually one eye at a time, with a gap of a few days to weeks.

### 6\. How soon can I use my phone after surgery?

Light use is allowed from the next day.

In selected cases it improves precision, but conventional phaco is equally effective in most patients.

### 8\. Will I need glasses after cataract surgery?

Depends on lens type chosen.

## 👁️ Understanding the Difference Between LASIK and ICL

### LASIK

* Reshapes the cornea
* Removes corneal tissue
* Permanent structural change

👉 LASIK surgery: <https://www.eyesurgeonmumbai.com/lasik-surgery-mumbai>

### ICL

* A biocompatible lens implanted inside the eye
* No corneal tissue removal
* Reversible procedure

👉 ICL surgery[https://](https://www.eyesurgeonmumbai.com/icl-surgery-mumbai)[www.eyesurgeonmumbai.com/icl-surgery-mumbai](http://www.eyesurgeonmumbai.com/icl-surgery-mumbai)

The choice depends on anatomy and safety.   

## 🧠 When ICL Is Safer Than LASIK

### 1\. High Myopia

If power is very high:

* LASIK may require excessive corneal thinning
* Risk of long-term corneal weakness increases

ICL can correct high power without removing corneal tissue.

### 2\. Thin Corneas

LASIK requires adequate corneal thickness.If the cornea is thin:

* LASIK may weaken structural stability
* Risk of ectasia increases

Dr. Nikhil Nasta prioritises long-term corneal health.

### 3\. Dry Eye Disease

LASIK can temporarily worsen dry eye.

In patients with:

* Chronic dry eye
* Meibomian gland dysfunction
* Screen-related dryness

ICL may preserve surface comfort better.

👉 Dry eye treatment[https://](https://www.eyesurgeonmumbai.com/dry-eye-treatment-mumbai)[www.eyesurgeonmumbai.com/dry-eye-treatment-mumbai](http://www.eyesurgeonmumbai.com/dry-eye-treatment-mumbai)

### 4\. Borderline Corneal Topography

Irregular corneal maps may increase LASIK risk.

ICL does not alter the cornea, making it safer in such cases.

### 5\. Desire for Reversibility

ICL:

* Can be removed if needed
* Preserves corneal structure

This reassures some patients.   

## 🔬 Is ICL More Invasive Than LASIK?

ICL is:

* An internal lens implantation
* Done through a small incision
* Quick and predictable

Though it sounds more invasive, modern ICL surgery is highly refined and safe when performed by experienced surgeons.

Many ICL patients report:

* Sharper vision
* Better contrast

* Excellent night vision

Dr. Nikhil Nasta explains that visual outcomes often depend on individual anatomy rather than procedure popularity.   

## 🧪 Is ICL Riskier Than LASIK?

Both are safe when correctly indicated.

The real risk lies in:

* Choosing LASIK for the wrong cornea
* Ignoring high myopia
* Overcorrecting thin corneas

At I-Sight Eye Care, safety dictates the recommendation.

## 📘 Introduction

Night driving is one of the biggest concerns patients have before choosing a premium intraocular lens. Many have heard stories of halos, starbursts, or glare after lens implantation.

So what is the truth about EDOF lenses?   

At **I-Sight Eye Care**, **Dr. Nikhil Nasta** carefully explains the optical differences between EDOF and multifocal lenses so patients make informed decisions.   

## 👁️ Why Halos and Glare Happen After Lens Surgery

Halos and glare occur due to how light is processed inside the eye.

With certain premium lenses:

* Light is split into multiple focal points
* This can reduce contrast
* Night light sources may appear as rings

This is more common in multifocal lenses.   

## 🔬 How EDOF Lenses Are Different

EDOF lenses:

* Extend the depth of focus
* Do not aggressively split light
* Maintain better contrast sensitivity

👉 EDOF IOL surgery: <https://www.eyesurgeonmumbai.com/edof-iol-surgery-mumbai>

Dr. Nikhil Nasta explains that because light is handled differently, visual disturbances are generally milder.   

## 🌙 Do EDOF Lenses Cause Halos?

Possible, but typically:

* Mild
* Temporary
* Less frequent than multifocal lenses

Most patients adapt within weeks to months.   

## 🚗 Are EDOF Lenses Good for Night Driving?

Yes, especially compared to multifocal lenses.

Benefits include:

* Better contrast
* Reduced starbursts
* More natural visual experience
* Greater comfort during highway driving

At I-Sight Eye Care, lens choice always considers driving habits.   

## 🧠 Who Is Most Sensitive to Halos?

Patients who:

* Drive frequently at night
* Have large pupils
* Are highly detail-oriented
* Have mild dry eye
* Have corneal irregularities

Dr. Nikhil Nasta evaluates these factors before recommending EDOF or trifocal lenses.

## ⭐ Featured Snippet Answer

According to **Dr. Nikhil Nasta of I-Sight Eye Care**, a cataract cannot come back once it has been surgically removed. However, some patients may develop posterior capsule opacification, often called secondary cataract, which can cause blurry vision and is easily treated with a quick YAG laser procedure at I-Sight Eye Care.

![](https://static.wixstatic.com/media/1231c0_895f13ec4a454352a450e40eb6500688~mv2.png/v1/fill/w_49,h_37,al_c,q_85,usm_0.66_1.00_0.01,blur_2,enc_avif,quality_auto/1231c0_895f13ec4a454352a450e40eb6500688~mv2.png)

## 📘 Introduction

Many patients who notice blurred vision months or years after cataract surgery worry that the cataract has returned.

The good news is that **a true cataract cannot grow back** once removed. But there is a common condition that can mimic its symptoms.

At **I-Sight Eye Care**, **Dr. Nikhil Nasta** explains this clearly so patients understand what is happening inside the eye.   

## 👁️ Why Cataract Cannot Return

During cataract surgery:

* The cloudy natural lens is removed
* A clear artificial intraocular lens is implanted

Since the natural lens is removed permanently, it cannot become cloudy again.

👉 Cataract surgery: <https://www.eyesurgeonmumbai.com/cataract-surgery-mumbai>   

## 🧠 Then Why Does Vision Become Blurry Again?

The most common reason is **Posterior Capsule Opacification**, also known as secondary cataract.   

## 🔬 What Is Posterior Capsule Opacification?

When cataract surgery is performed:

* The back layer of the lens capsule is left intact
* The artificial lens sits inside this capsule

Over time, cells can grow on this capsule and make it cloudy.

This cloudiness:

* Feels like cataract returning
* Causes blurred or hazy vision
* May cause glare at night

Dr. Nikhil Nasta reassures patients that this is common and treatable.   

## ⏳ How Soon Can Secondary Cataract Develop?

It may occur:

* Within months
* Or years after surgery
* In some patients never

There is no fixed timeline.   

## 🚨 Symptoms of Secondary Cataract

Patients may notice:

* Gradual blurring of vision
* Glare from lights
* Reduced contrast
* Difficulty reading

These symptoms are similar to original cataract but easier to treat.   

## 🛠️ How Is Secondary Cataract Treated?

Treatment is done using a **YAG laser capsulotomy**.

This procedure:

* Takes only a few minutes
* Is painless
* Does not require stitches
* Restores clarity quickly
* Is done as an outpatient procedure

At I-Sight Eye Care, YAG laser treatment is performed safely and efficiently.   

## 👁️ Is YAG Laser Safe?

According to Dr. Nikhil Nasta:

* YAG laser is very safe
* Complication risk is minimal
* Vision often improves immediately

Most patients resume normal activities the same day.   

## 🧠 Can Secondary Cataract Happen More Than Once?

No.

Once the cloudy capsule is opened with YAG laser, it does not grow back again.   

## 👨‍⚕️ How Dr. Nikhil Nasta Handles Post-Cataract Vision Changes

At I-Sight Eye Care:

* Regular follow-ups detect capsule clouding early
* YAG laser is performed only when needed
* Retina is evaluated before and after treatment
* Patients are counselled clearly

This ensures smooth long-term vision after cataract surgery.   

## 🏁 Conclusion

A cataract cannot come back after surgery. However, posterior capsule opacification can cause similar symptoms and is easily treatable with a quick laser procedure.

Under the care of **Dr. Nikhil Nasta at I-Sight Eye Care**, patients receive complete post-cataract care to maintain long-term clear vision.

No. The natural lens is permanently removed.

### What is secondary cataract?

## ⭐ Featured Snippet Answer

According to **Dr. Nikhil Nasta of I-Sight Eye Care**, eye floaters are common after the age of 40 and are usually related to natural age related changes inside the eye. However, sudden onset, increase in floaters, flashes of light, or vision loss require urgent retinal evaluation.

  
## 📘 Introduction

Many people notice small moving spots, threads, or shadows in their vision after the age of 40\. These are called **eye floaters**.

Most floaters are harmless. But some can signal serious retinal problems.

At **I-Sight Eye Care**, **Dr. Nikhil Nasta** helps patients distinguish between normal ageing changes and floaters that need urgent attention.

  
![](https://static.wixstatic.com/media/1231c0_04050ed4c5294b3b85c23279982063cd~mv2.png/v1/fill/w_49,h_37,al_c,q_85,usm_0.66_1.00_0.01,blur_2,enc_avif,quality_auto/1231c0_04050ed4c5294b3b85c23279982063cd~mv2.png)

  
## 👁️ What Exactly Are Eye Floaters?

Eye floaters are tiny clumps or strands inside the vitreous gel of the eye.

They may appear as:

* Dots
* Threads
* Cobweb like shapes
* Moving shadows

They drift as the eyes move and are more visible against bright backgrounds.   

## 🧠 Why Floaters Become Common After 40

As we age:

* The vitreous gel becomes more liquid
* Microscopic fibres clump together
* These cast shadows on the retina

This process is called **posterior vitreous detachment**, and it is common after 40.

Dr. Nikhil Nasta explains that **most age related floaters are benign**.   

## ✅ When Eye Floaters Are Considered Normal

Floaters are usually normal if:

* They appear gradually
* They are few in number
* There are no flashes of light
* Vision remains clear
* They do not worsen rapidly

At I-Sight Eye Care, such floaters are monitored rather than treated aggressively.   

## 🚨 Warning Signs That Need Immediate Eye Check

Seek urgent evaluation if you notice:

* Sudden shower of floaters
* Bright flashes of light
* Curtain or shadow in vision
* Sudden vision loss
* One eye affected suddenly

These can indicate:

* Retinal tear
* Retinal detachment
* Vitreous hemorrhage

👉 Retina services: <https://www.eyesurgeonmumbai.com/retinalsurgerymumbai>

Dr. Nikhil Nasta stresses that **early treatment can save vision**.   

## 👁️ Are Floaters Linked to Serious Eye Disease?

Sometimes, yes.

Floaters may be associated with:

* Retinal tears
* Retinal detachment
* High myopia
* Diabetes related eye disease
* Eye trauma

This is why a proper retinal examination is essential.   

## 🩺 How Eye Floaters Are Evaluated at I-Sight Eye Care

Assessment includes:

* Dilated retinal examination
* Vitreous evaluation
* Retinal imaging if needed
* Monitoring for progression

Dr. Nikhil Nasta ensures no retinal pathology is missed.   

## 🧪 Can Eye Floaters Be Treated?

Most floaters:

* Fade over time
* Become less noticeable
* Do not require treatment

Treatment is considered only when:

* Floaters severely affect vision
* There is underlying retinal disease

Reassurance and monitoring are often the best approach.

## 🧠 Can Eye Floaters Be Prevented?

Age related floaters cannot be prevented, but:

* Regular eye exams help early detection
* Good diabetic control reduces retinal risk
* Protective eyewear prevents trauma

At I-Sight Eye Care, preventive eye care is strongly encouraged after 40.   

## 👨‍⚕️ Dr. Nikhil Nasta’s Advice on Eye Floaters

Dr. Nikhil Nasta advises:

* Do not ignore sudden changes
* Do not panic over stable floaters
* Get a baseline eye exam after 40
* Seek urgent care if warning signs appear

## 🏁 Conclusion

Eye floaters are common after the age of 40 and are usually harmless. However, sudden or severe changes should never be ignored.

Under the care of **Dr. Nikhil Nasta at I-Sight Eye Care**, patients receive thorough retinal evaluation and clear guidance on when floaters are normal and when they are not.

## ❓ FAQs

### Are eye floaters normal after 40?

Yes, most are age related and harmless.

### Do floaters go away on their own?

Many become less noticeable over time.

### Can floaters cause blindness?

Not directly, but associated retinal conditions can if untreated.

### Should floaters always be checked?

Yes, especially if sudden or increasing.

## ⭐ Featured Snippet Answer

According to **Dr. Nikhil Nasta of I-Sight Eye Care**, glaucoma can exist for years without any noticeable symptoms. At I-Sight Eye Care, many patients are diagnosed during routine eye exams, which is why regular screening is critical to prevent irreversible vision loss.   

![](https://static.wixstatic.com/media/1231c0_b3a1e01730a342b59f664c96a582ef5c~mv2.png/v1/fill/w_49,h_37,al_c,q_85,usm_0.66_1.00_0.01,blur_2,enc_avif,quality_auto/1231c0_b3a1e01730a342b59f664c96a582ef5c~mv2.png)

## 📘 Introduction

Glaucoma is one of the leading causes of irreversible blindness worldwide. What makes it especially dangerous is that **most patients do not feel anything wrong in the early stages**.

At **I-Sight Eye Care**, **Dr. Nikhil Nasta** often diagnoses glaucoma in patients who came in for routine eye checkups and had no visual complaints at all.

## 👁️ Why Glaucoma Is Called the Silent Thief of Vision

Glaucoma typically:

* Progresses slowly
* Damages peripheral vision first
* Preserves central vision until late stages
* Causes no pain in most cases

Because daily vision feels normal, patients assume their eyes are healthy.

## 🧠 Can You Really Have Glaucoma Without Symptoms?

Yes.

In early and moderate stages:

* Vision appears clear
* Reading is unaffected
* No redness or pain
* No obvious warning signs

Dr. Nikhil Nasta explains that **by the time symptoms appear, vision loss is often advanced and permanent**.

## 🚨 When Symptoms Finally Appear

Late-stage glaucoma may cause:

* Tunnel vision
* Difficulty seeing at night
* Bumping into objects
* Vision loss from the sides

At this stage, treatment can only prevent further damage, not restore lost vision.

## 🧪 Who Is at Higher Risk for Silent Glaucoma?

You are at higher risk if you:

* Are over 40 years of age
* Have a family history of glaucoma
* Have diabetes or high blood pressure
* Have high eye pressure
* Are highly myopic
* Use steroid medications long term

👉 Glaucoma services[https://](https://www.eyesurgeonmumbai.com/glaucoma-treatment-mumbai)[www.eyesurgeonmumbai.com/glaucoma-treatment-mumbai](http://www.eyesurgeonmumbai.com/glaucoma-treatment-mumbai)

Dr. Nikhil Nasta recommends proactive screening in these groups.

## 👁️ Types of Glaucoma That Are Usually Symptomless

### Primary Open Angle Glaucoma

* Most common type
* Progresses silently
* Diagnosed on screening

### Normal Tension Glaucoma

* Eye pressure may be normal
* Nerve damage still occurs

These forms highlight why pressure alone is not enough to rule out glaucoma.

## 🩺 How Glaucoma Is Detected at I-Sight Eye Care

Evaluation includes:

* Eye pressure measurement
* Optic nerve examination
* Visual field testing
* OCT nerve fibre analysis
* Corneal thickness measurement

This comprehensive approach allows early diagnosis.

## 🛑 Why Early Detection Matters

Once optic nerve damage occurs:

* Vision loss is irreversible
* Treatment focuses on slowing progression

Early diagnosis:

* Preserves remaining vision
* Prevents disability
* Protects long-term independence

Dr. Nikhil Nasta emphasises that **glaucoma blindness is preventable with early care**.

## 👨‍⚕️ Dr. Nikhil Nasta’s Glaucoma Philosophy

At I-Sight Eye Care:

* Glaucoma is treated as a lifelong condition
* Regular monitoring is essential
* Treatment plans are individualised
* Patient education is prioritised

## 🏁 Conclusion

Yes, glaucoma can exist completely without symptoms, which is what makes it dangerous. Routine eye exams are the only reliable way to detect it early and protect vision.

Under the care of **Dr. Nikhil Nasta at I-Sight Eye Care**, patients receive comprehensive glaucoma screening and long-term vision protection.

## ❓ FAQs

### Can glaucoma exist without pain?

Yes. Most forms of glaucoma are painless.

### Can glaucoma be cured?

No. It can be controlled but not reversed.

### Is glaucoma common after 40?

Yes. Risk increases with age.

### How often should glaucoma screening be done?

As advised by your ophthalmologist based on risk.

![](https://static.wixstatic.com/media/1231c0_9b0417b0878241b69edb867ddd3063f9~mv2.png/v1/fill/w_49,h_37,al_c,q_85,usm_0.66_1.00_0.01,blur_2,enc_avif,quality_auto/1231c0_9b0417b0878241b69edb867ddd3063f9~mv2.png)

  
## 📘 Introduction

Many patients notice that their vision becomes blurry, fluctuates during the day, or clears after blinking. This often raises an alarming question“Is my blurry vision permanent?”

Dry eye disease is one of the **most underdiagnosed causes of fluctuating vision**. At **I-Sight Eye Care**, **Dr. Nikhil Nasta** regularly sees patients who fear permanent vision loss due to untreated dry eye.   

## 👁️ How Dry Eye Causes Blurry Vision

Clear vision depends on a stable tear film. Dry eye disrupts this layer.

When tears are inadequate or unstable:

* Light entering the eye scatters
* Vision becomes hazy
* Clarity fluctuates during blinking
* Screens worsen symptoms

Dr. Nikhil Nasta explains that **dry eye affects vision quality, not eye power**.   

## 🧠 Is Blurry Vision From Dry Eye Permanent?

### In Most Cases

No. Blurry vision from dry eye is usually **reversible** when treated early.

### In Long-Standing Untreated Dry Eye

It can lead to:

* Chronic corneal surface inflammation
* Irregular tear film
* Persistent visual fluctuation
* Reduced visual comfort

Permanent vision loss is rare, but **long-term visual instability** can occur without treatment.   

## 🚨 Signs Dry Eye Is Affecting Vision Seriously

You should seek evaluation if:

* Vision clears after blinking
* Vision worsens with screen use
* Eyes feel gritty or burning
* Redness persists
* Artificial tears give only short relief

👉 Dry eye treatment: <https://www.eyesurgeonmumbai.com/dry-eye-treatment-mumbai>

At I-Sight Eye Care, advanced diagnostics identify dry eye severity accurately.   

## 🧪 Types of Dry Eye and Visual Impact

### Evaporative Dry Eye

* Common in screen users
* Tear film breaks quickly
* Vision fluctuates more

### Aqueous Deficient Dry Eye

* Less tear production
* Persistent blur and discomfort

Dr. Nikhil Nasta tailors treatment based on the type, not just symptoms.   

## 💻 Why Screens Make Dry Eye Vision Worse

Screens reduce blink rate, causing:

* Faster tear evaporation
* Increased blur
* Eye strain

This is why many patients report clearer vision in the morning and worsening blur by evening.   

## 🩺 How Dry Eye Is Diagnosed at I-Sight Eye Care

Evaluation includes:

* Tear film assessment
* Meibomian gland evaluation
* Corneal surface examination
* Blink pattern analysis

This medical approach prevents misdiagnosis and ineffective treatment.   

## 🧠 Can Dry Eye Mimic Other Eye Problems?

Yes. Dry eye can mimic:

* Eye power changes
* Cataract symptoms
* Post LASIK blur

Dr. Nikhil Nasta always rules out dry eye before changing glasses or planning surgery.   

## 🛠️ Treatment Prevents Long-Term Vision Problems

Treatment may include:

* Targeted lubricants
* Eyelid hygiene
* Meibomian gland therapy
* IPL for chronic dry eye
* Lifestyle and screen habit correction

Early treatment prevents progression and restores stable vision.   

## 👨‍⚕️ Dr. Nikhil Nasta’s Approach to Dry Eye

At I-Sight Eye Care:

* Dry eye is treated as a medical disease
* Root cause is identified
* Long-term control is planned
* Vision quality is prioritised

## 🏁 Conclusion

Dry eye rarely causes permanent vision loss, but it can cause long-term visual disturbance if ignored. The good news is that with timely treatment, vision stability can be restored.

Under the care of **Dr. Nikhil Nasta at I-Sight Eye Care**, patients receive comprehensive dry eye care that protects both comfort and vision.

Rarely, but long-term untreated dry eye can cause persistent visual disturbance.

## 📘 Introduction

Many people in their 40s consider LASIK but hesitate because they hear statements like“LASIK is only for young people” or “LASIK does not work after 40.”

The truth is more nuanced.

  
At **I-Sight Eye Care**, **Dr. Nikhil Nasta** regularly evaluates patients over 40 for vision correction and helps them choose the safest and most effective option based on eye health and long-term needs.   

## 👁️ Why LASIK After 40 Raises Questions

After the age of 40, natural changes begin in the eyes, including:

* Reduced near focusing ability
* Early presbyopia
* Higher dry eye tendency
* Changes in lens flexibility

These factors do not automatically rule out LASIK, but they **change the decision-making process**.   

## 🧠 What Changes in Vision After 40?

### Presbyopia Begins

Presbyopia is the age-related loss of near focusing ability.

Important to understand:

* LASIK reshapes the cornea
* Presbyopia occurs inside the natural lens
* LASIK does not stop presbyopia

Dr. Nikhil Nasta explains this clearly so expectations remain realistic.   

## ✅ When LASIK Can Be Safe After 40

LASIK may be a good option if:

* Eye power is stable
* Cornea thickness is adequate
* Dry eye is mild and controlled
* No early cataract is present
* Patient understands reading glasses may still be needed

👉 LASIK services: <https://www.eyesurgeonmumbai.com/lasik-surgery-mumbai>

At I-Sight Eye Care, detailed pre-LASIK screening ensures safety.   

## 🚫 When LASIK May Not Be the Best Option After 40

LASIK may not be advised if:

* Presbyopia is the main concern
* Dry eye is significant
* Early cataract is developing
* Corneal thickness is borderline
* Patient expects complete freedom from reading glasses

In such cases, alternatives may give better long-term satisfaction.   

## 🔄 Better Alternatives to LASIK After 40

### **1\. Monovision LASIK**

One eye corrected for distance, the other for near.

* Suitable for select patients
* Requires careful trial and counselling

### **2\. Lens-Based Vision Correction**

In patients with early lens changes:

* Cataract or refractive lens exchange may be better
* Allows use of EDOF or multifocal lenses

👉 Cataract surgery: <https://www.eyesurgeonmumbai.com/cataract-surgery-mumbai>   

👉 EDOF IOLs: <https://www.eyesurgeonmumbai.com/edof-iol-surgery-mumbai>   

Dr. Nikhil Nasta often recommends lens-based solutions when LASIK would be short-lived.

## 👁️ Dry Eye Considerations After 40

Dry eye becomes more common with age.

Important points:

* LASIK can temporarily worsen dry eye
* Existing dry eye must be treated first
* Long-term comfort matters more than speed

👉 Dry eye treatment: <https://www.eyesurgeonmumbai.com/dry-eye-treatment-mumbai>

At I-Sight Eye Care, dry eye is always addressed before refractive surgery.

Evaluation includes:

* Detailed corneal mapping
* Tear film analysis
* Lens clarity assessment
* Lifestyle discussion

This ensures the chosen procedure remains beneficial for years, not just months.   

## 🏁 Conclusion

LASIK can be safe after the age of 40, but it is not a one-size-fits-all solution. The real question is not age, but whether LASIK is the **right solution for the stage your eyes are in**.
